[2018-04-11 16:56:59] Koreksi BCC STEP 4 : 
									SELECT 
										CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
										AS NO_REKAP_BCC
									FROM (
										SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
										FROM (
											SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
											FROM (  
												SELECT *
												FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												WHERE ID_RENCANA = '20180405.MANUAL.41/4121/0217/4239'
												AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O370'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC
											) a
										)
										WHERE rown = 1
									)

[2018-04-11 17:19:22] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O377'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:19:47] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O377'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:20:21] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O377'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:20:53] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *

[2018-04-11 17:21:43] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O377'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:22:47] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O377'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:24:48] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O377'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:24:58] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O377'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:27:16] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O376'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:30:11] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O376'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O379'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O379'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-11 17:36:41] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122O379'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC

								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180410.MANUAL.41/4121/0111/45'

												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1

											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
